// Dota2 Editor

"DOTAAbilities"
{

	// 没有用无敌，因为很多情况下要给单位添加modifier，如果单位无敌，虽然可以通过设置modifier的属性使单位拥有modifier，但是modifier的一些特性会失效（比如在创建的时候给单位添加特效就不会生效），所以使用攻击免疫和魔免（魔抗100%，但是不免疫技能）来实现无敌效果，同时为了避免纯粹伤害（暂时没有）影响，最小生命值设置为1点
	"dummy_unit"
	{
		"BaseClass"	"ability_datadriven"
		"AbilityBehavior"	"DOTA_ABILITY_BEHAVIOR_HIDDEN | DOTA_ABILITY_BEHAVIOR_PASSIVE"
		"precache"
		{
			"particle"	"particles/generic_gameplay/screen_arcane_drop.vpcf"
		}
		"Modifiers"
		{
			"modifier_dummy_unit"
			{
				"Passive"	"1"
				"IsHidden"	"1"
				"States"
				{
					"MODIFIER_STATE_NO_HEALTH_BAR"	"MODIFIER_STATE_VALUE_ENABLED"
					"MODIFIER_STATE_NOT_ON_MINIMAP"	"MODIFIER_STATE_VALUE_ENABLED"
					"MODIFIER_STATE_NO_UNIT_COLLISION"	"MODIFIER_STATE_VALUE_ENABLED"
					"MODIFIER_STATE_ATTACK_IMMUNE"	"MODIFIER_STATE_VALUE_ENABLED"
					"MODIFIER_STATE_MAGIC_IMMUNE"	"MODIFIER_STATE_VALUE_ENABLED"
				}
				"Properties"	{}
			}
			"modifier_dummy_unit_health"
			{
				"IsHidden"	"1"
				"Properties"
				{
					"MODIFIER_PROPERTY_MIN_HEALTH"	"1"
				}
				"Passive"	"1"
			}
			"modifier_dummy_unit_select"
			{
				"Passive"	"1"
				"States"
				{
					"MODIFIER_STATE_UNSELECTABLE"	"MODIFIER_STATE_VALUE_ENABLED"
				}
				"IsHidden"	"1"
			}
			"modifier_dummy_unit_move"
			{
				"Passive"	"1"
				"States"
				{
					"MODIFIER_STATE_ROOTED"	"MODIFIER_STATE_VALUE_ENABLED"
				}
				"IsHidden"	"1"
			}
		}
	}

	// 第一个buff是一个法球效果，只是为了覆盖掉攻击投射物。直接在法球buff里面的法球命中处理的话，会导致出现两次法球，应该是法球还没命中，第二次攻击就开始了，导致又出现了一个法球。因此法球发射的时候，添加damage这个buff，以实现攻击效果，同时移除掉法球效果，这样就只会有一次效果了
	"mhj_JiNing_myzjjd_wx"
	{
		"BaseClass"	"ability_datadriven"
		"AbilityTextureName"	"custom/明月终极剑道-第二式"
		"AbilityBehavior"	"DOTA_ABILITY_BEHAVIOR_NO_TARGET | DOTA_ABILITY_BEHAVIOR_IGNORE_BACKSWING"
		"AbilityUnitTargetType"	"DOTA_UNIT_TARGET_HERO | DOTA_UNIT_TARGET_BASIC"
		"AbilityUnitTargetTeam"	"DOTA_UNIT_TARGET_TEAM_FRIENDLY"
		"MaxLevel"	"0"
		"AbilityCastAnimation"	"ACT_DOTA_ATTACK"
		"AbilityCooldown"	"2.5"
		"precache"
		{
			"particle"	"particles/units/heroes/hero_templar_assassin/templar_assassin_meld_attack.vpcf"
			"particle"	"particles/items3_fx/star_emblem_brokenshield_caster.vpcf"
			"soundfile"	"soundevents/game_sounds_heroes/game_sounds_templar_assassin.vsndevts"
		}
		"OnSpellStart"
		{
			"ApplyModifier"
			{
				"Target"	"CASTER"
				"ModifierName"	"modifier_mhj_JiNing_myzjjd_wx"
			}
		}
		"Modifiers"
		{
			"modifier_mhj_JiNing_myzjjd_wx"
			{
				"IsBuff"	"1"
				"Orb"
				{
					"Priority"	"DOTA_ORB_PRIORITY_ABILITY"
					"ProjectileName"	"particles/units/heroes/hero_templar_assassin/templar_assassin_meld_attack.vpcf"
				}
				"OnOrbFire"
				{
					"ApplyModifier"
					{
						"Target"	"CASTER"

					}
					"RemoveModifier"

			{
				"IsDebuff"	"1"

					}
				}

				{
					"RunScript"
					{
						"ScriptFile"	"scripts/vscripts/abilities/common.lua"

				}

			{
				"IsHidden"	"1"
				"OnAttackLanded"
				{
					"FireSound"
